27 Jun 2015

Obfuscated code from the WordPress hack

This page is part of the blogpost About that time I dealt with a bunch of hackers on a WordPress.

The following is an example of the code I found when one of the WordPress installations I managed was hacked. You can find the deobfuscated version right over here.

$indkcf="base64_decode";return $indkcf($r);}
